**FAQ:**
- **Q: Is NPP the same as Deca-Durabolin?** A: NPP and Deca both contain the same active hormone (Nandrolone), but attached to different esters. - **Q: Why choose NPP over Deca?** A: NPP is preferred for shorter cycles (8–10 weeks), when you want effects within the first week, or when faster PCT initiation is important. - **Q: Can I inject NPP less frequently than EOD?** A: Every 3 days (E3D) is acceptable but not optimal. EOD injections maintain the most stable blood levels with the Phenylpropionate ester. Less frequent injection leads to fluctuations that can increase side effects. The trade-off for NPP's fast onset and clearance is more frequent pinning.

Supplementing T3 overrides this adaptive response, maintaining elevated metabolism even deep into a cut. This is why competitive preps that include T3 produce consistently leaner results.
- **Q: What's the best T3 + Clen stack protocol?** A: Run T3 at 50mcg/day continuously (with proper taper at end), and cycle Clen 2 weeks on / 2 weeks off at 80–120mcg. During Clen off-weeks, T3 maintains elevated metabolism. During Clen on-weeks, both compounds synergise for maximum thermogenic effect. Always combine with AAS (minimum TRT testosterone).
- **Q: How long can I safely run T3?** A: Most athletes run T3 for 6–12 weeks during contest prep. Extended runs beyond 12 weeks increase the risk of temporary thyroid suppression that takes longer to recover from. Always taper over 2 weeks minimum. With proper tapering, thyroid function typically normalises within 4–6 weeks post-discontinuation.
